# 第16回 サンプル実験

## Sample: RLC共振（RK4）

### Code
```c
#include <stdio.h>

/*
  RLC直列回路（自由振動）の状態方程式（Vin=0）
    di/dt  = -(R/L) i - (1/L) Vc
    dVc/dt = (1/C) i
  状態 x = [ i, Vc ]
*/

typedef struct {
  double i;
  double vc;
} State;

State f(State x, double R, double L, double C) {
  State dx;
  dx.i  = -(R / L) * x.i - (1.0 / L) * x.vc;
  dx.vc = (1.0 / C) * x.i;
  return dx;
}

State add(State a, State b, double k) {
  State y;
  y.i  = a.i  + k * b.i;
  y.vc = a.vc + k * b.vc;
  return y;
}

State rk4_step(State x, double dt, double R, double L, double C) {
  State k1 = f(x, R, L, C);
  State k2 = f(add(x, k1, dt / 2), R, L, C);
  State k3 = f(add(x, k2, dt / 2), R, L, C);
  State k4 = f(add(x, k3, dt),   R, L, C);

  State next;
  next.i  = x.i  + (dt / 6) * (k1.i  + 2 * k2.i  + 2 * k3.i  + k4.i);
  next.vc = x.vc + (dt / 6) * (k1.vc + 2 * k2.vc + 2 * k3.vc + k4.vc);
  return next;
}

int main(void) {
  double R = 10.0, L = 0.01, C = 0.0001;
  double dt = 0.0001;
  int steps = 2000;

  State x;
  x.vc = 5.0;  // Vc(0)
  x.i  = 0.0;  // i(0)

  for (int n = 0; n <= steps; n++) {
    double t = n * dt;
    printf("%f,%f,%f\n", t, x.i, x.vc);  // CSV: t,i,Vc
    x = rk4_step(x, dt, R, L, C);
  }
  return 0;
}
```

- n
